--- 帖子 #1904 ---
I started trading this EA on a demo account a few weeks ago. Overall, the results have been mixed. I have now stopped testing the EA for the following reasons :-

a) There appear to be some bugs in the EA eg double trades, move to BE not working all the time, cancel opposite orders not always working.

b) The results showed considerable volatility even in a short space of time. This would suggest profit being heavily reliant upon time in the cycle and hence risky ie potential for large drawdown.

c) The original key developer and contributors to this EA don't seem around anymore. This raises a red flag.

That said ... I spent a good deal of time reading through the entire thread, testing etc. However, this is clearly only a fraction of the time spent on this by the originators of the theory, EA developers and early testers. If indeed the EA has proven unviable, this is a huge shame.

Sincere thanks and respect to all involved. If I am right that this EA has not fulfilled everyone's expectations, I hope this will not deter others from working on new strategies. On the contrary, the lesson we can all take from this is how long it takes to prove a winning strategy, the amount of work involved and the caution required prior to trading live.

Cav

--- 帖子 #1923 ---
Hi tomomi72003, I had been recommended a larger SL for this method by a very good trader many weeks ago. However, I failed to listen,"and did it my way." It looks now to me that a SL of 45-60 pips on Eur/Usd may produce better results. Testing with IBFX strategy tester from 3/09/08 to 8/08/08 produced good results in my opinion. My settings were : Margin...6. SL...45. Break even...20. TP 1...20. TP 2...30. TP 3...55. Day/Start/Hour...1 hour before London open. After time change in London, this is 06:00 GMT, then reverts to 07:00 when time is changed back. Look Back Hours...24. Order Expiration Hours...9. I have orders expiring one hour before London close. Of course this is not trading advice. It is just how I have tested the method. Of course it must be remembered that MT4 strategy testers have been called second rate, and also that one should not place a great deal of faith in their output, because they are not tick by tick data. I am not too sure about this. Anyway, good luck in your trading.

Daily candles are the same all over the world, isn't it?

In my opinion, working on daily candles take the work easier.

Another point: I'm trying to define take profit levels in this way.

Take profit 1: High[1] + 15% previous day ATR(4)

Take profit 2: High[1] + 30% previous day ATR(4)

Take profit 3: High[1] + 45% previous day ATR(4)

In recent months I read some breakout systems studies and I saw that the ATR(4) instead of ATR(14) or ATR(21) works very well on a small time horizon.

I will post here if I obtain interesting results.

i've tasted this system many times, its always make you lose pips what means money,

there is an idea cames to my head that night when i was thinking of this system, its a gamblers way of getting rich, and i think you can apply it here and profit too..

use a little % of your whole capetal, just like %1, and X2 it when you lose.

Exampel-

in $10,000 account..

first day you lost 100 pips what means $100  thats %1 of your account.

2nd day you enter with $200 what means %2 of ur account, if you win 100 pips then you have made %1 profit in 2 days, if you lost the %2 again in the 2nd day.

then the 3rd day come, you enter with %4 of your account, if you win 100 pips then you have made %1 profit in 3 days, if you lost the %4 then enter with %8 in the 4th day

its kinda easy money management strategy, and it can low the risk..

there is another thing important, that your first entary is what you will get after the end of the lossing wave, exampel, when u first enter with $1000, and got 10 losses in row in 10 days, and won in the 11 day, that means you have made $1000 in 11 days, if you entered with $10, and again got into 10 lossing trades in row, and won in the 11 day that means you have made just $10 in 11 days. so its matter how much money you have in ur account since you just ganna use %1 or %2 of ur whole capetal.

another thing, you need to TP the same amount of pips if u wanna use this money management strategy.

thanks for reading, for more information feel free to PM me

Faris.

--- 帖子 #1933 ---
The system you are referring to is called Martingale system and it's nothing new.

You forgot to mention one tiny rhing, but it's a huge thing.

If you had 10000$, and first day you started with 10% (100$), let's look what would happen if you would double every day (if we have a loosing streak)

1 day -  100$  (100$ total invested)

2 day -  200$  (300$ total)

3 day -  400$  (700$)

4 day -  800$  (1500$)

5 day - 1600$ (3100$)

6 day - 3200$ (6300$)

7 day - 6400$ (12700$)

So, as you see, you would not last for more than 6 days with this system.

8 day - 12800$ (25500$)

9 day - 25600$ (51100$)

10 day - 51200$ (102300$)

As you also see, for 10 days you wouldn't survive even if you started with 1% (10$) !

Yes I'm still trading this or a slight variation.  I'm just using a single order on GBP/JPY.

Start time 7am BST

Stop 60

Its fairly robust for this pair as other parameters work well.  Other pairs are also profitable but to a lesser extent.

If you can handle the drawdowns higher profit targets are more profitable, but I'm happy with a conservative setting for now.

--- 帖子 #1941 ---
The back test does not consider spread but I don't see the spread impact being significant.

The way I view spread is as follows:-

The spread on my spread betting account is 8 pips for gbp/jpy so there are 4 pips either side of the 'target' buy/sell price.

So basically my orders are placed 4 pips early and closed 4 pips late. The spread would only be important when:-

1. My order is filled and price then reverses to stop me out without reaching the target order price (which is 4 pips away)

2. A filled order hits the profit target price but then reverses to be stopped out without hitting the bid/offer price for the progit to be filled (which is 4 pips away)

On these 2 occaisons losses would have occured in real trading but not in the back test.

These will be offset by the opposite happeneing with the stop loss price.

The occaisons above will have happened during the test but they will not be very often.  For all other trades the backtest would be as per real trading.

I hope I've made this easy to understand, I beleive I am right although stand to be corrected.

Cheers

Nick

--- 帖子 #1952 ---
You can place two limit orders at the same time. But you can't have 2 open trades if one is long and the other short... they would cancel each other out. So using this system you need to be aware if your buy and sells overlap. It could happen if the previous days trading had a high/low range of only say 20 pips.

--- 帖子 #1974 ---
Hi Shrips,

I cannot tell you why 17 hours particularly and I don't believe that it is particularly relevent. The whole breakout concept is to do with the Asian range.

Various people have written about price behavior in relation to it, Boris Schlossberg for one.

Phil Newton has another view and has his 'set of hours' from which he trades the breakout.

I have been looking at a half hour range just prior to Europe opening.

The real problem is the false breaks by an odd pip or two from any line selected. Add a ten pip buffer and you will see price go twelve pips, come back and hit your stop loss.

There are also commercial packages available 'London Rush' and another later version with a similar name.

Unfortunately none of these breakout systems just work!!

95 looked a good answer but until we find a way of dealing with the 'pop up and stops' it is not a long term winner.

--- 帖子 #1975 ---
I do like this system because of its high probability to reach TP(especially the first 2 TP) when the market is behaving in a strong trending  manner.

The key to trading this system long term is the ability to know when not to trade this. If you trade this 365 days of the year, I dont think you will show a profit.

Trade this in a week like we are having now and you will kill your account.

Just curious if anyone is trading this live and consistently showing good results?
